ğŸ“Š HAIROTICMEN â€“ PARTNER TYPES, LEVELS &amp; CONTRACTUAL SYSTEMğŸ§© 1. Partner Types Overview1. Handle Dealers (Retail B2B)   - Purchase products in moderate volume   - Resell in physical shops or online   - Entry-level discount and flexible terms2. Wholesalers / Distributors   - Purchase in bulk for regional resale   - May supply sub-retailers or salon chains   - Require larger volume and legal structure3. Exclusive Regional Partners   - Given exclusive city/region rights   - Must meet sales quota and represent brand   - High loyalty and co-branding support4. Salons / Barbershops (Salon Partners)   - Use and resell HAIROTICMEN in-salon   - Small orders with strong brand presence   - Receive display stands, samples, and materials5. Affiliates / Online Resellers   - Earn commission on referrals or online sales   - Must respect MSRP and approval policies   - Tracked using SliceWP system6. Sales Agents / Brand Ambassadors   - Work commission-based to introduce retailers   - Represent brand at events or markets   - Paid via affiliate-like system + bonusesğŸ“ˆ 2. Partner Programs AI Agent Documentation â€“ HAIROTICMENThis document defines the complete structure and behavior of the Partner Programs AI Agent for HAIROTICMEN. The agent operates under the centralized Hairo Assistant and manages dealers, stands, and affiliates, including loyalty points, rank/tiers, commissions, and rewards. It integrates with Odoo (partners, sales, accounting), WooCommerce (orders), myCred (loyalty), SliceWP (affiliates), Google Drive (policies &amp; logs), Monday.com (visibility), n8n (internal execution), Zapier (external communication), and MCP (governed access).1) Mission &amp; ScopeThe Partner Programs AI Agentâ€™s mission is to increase channel performance and loyalty by automating partner onboarding, calculating and awarding points/commissions, ensuring accurate payouts, and providing transparent dashboards to management. It covers three programs:â€¢ Dealers â€“ B2B resellers with volume pricing and tiered benefits.â€¢ Stands â€“ Point-of-sale partners (kiosks/booths) with stock &amp; sales tracking.â€¢ Affiliates â€“ Online promoters tracked via SliceWP with link-based attribution.2) Data Sources &amp; OwnershipAuthoritative systems:â€¢ Odoo ERP â€“ master record for partners (res.partner), pricelists, sales, invoices, and payouts.â€¢ myCred â€“ source-of-truth for loyalty points ledger (customers and partners).â€¢ SliceWP â€“ source-of-truth for affiliate referrals, conversion amounts, and payout status.â€¢ WooCommerce â€“ primary eCommerce orders; mirrored to Odoo for accounting.â€¢ Google Drive â€“ policies, tier matrices, payout reports, and audit logs.â€¢ Monday.com â€“ management dashboards (read-mostly).Ownership:â€¢ Financials, payouts, and partner ranking decisions are owned by Odoo.â€¢ Points ledger is owned by myCred; affiliate conversions by SliceWP.â€¢ AI writes only via MCP-scoped tools; all actions logged to Drive.3) Program Modelsâ€¢ Dealers (B2B):  â€“ Tiers: Bronze, Silver, Gold, Platinum (configurable in Drive /Partner_Policies/Tiers.xlsx).  â€“ Criteria: rolling 90-day revenue, order count, payment reliability.  â€“ Benefits: volume discounts (Odoo pricelists), expedited shipping, bonus points.  â€“ Reviews: automatic monthly tier evaluation.â€¢ Stands (POS Partners):  â€“ Inventory allocations tracked in Odoo (stock.picking to stand location).  â€“ Sales reconciliation weekly; points bonus for sell-through rate.  â€“ Service-level rules (display quality, return compliance) affect bonus.â€¢ Affiliates (SliceWP):  â€“ Attribution: last-click with 30-day cookie by default.  â€“ Commission: % of net order value excluding shipping/VAT (Drive /Partner_Policies/Commissions.xlsx).  â€“ Payment: monthly payout on approved conversions; disputes handled via ticketing.4) Event Triggersâ€¢ New partner registration (dealer/stand/affiliate).  â€¢ Order paid or delivered (WooCommerce â†’ Odoo).  â€¢ Affiliate conversion recorded/approved (SliceWP).  â€¢ Inventory transfer to stand (Odoo stock.picking).  â€¢ Monthly tier review and payout cycle.  â€¢ Manager queries to Hairo Assistant (â€œShow partner X pointsâ€, â€œCalculate commission due for Septemberâ€).  5) MCP Tools (Partner Catalog)â€¢ odoo.get_partner: Fetch partner (dealer/stand/affiliate) profile and status.â€¢ odoo.update_partner_tier: Set tier &amp; assign pricelist; record reason.â€¢ odoo.create_payout: Create payout entry (affiliate/dealer bonus) with external_id for idempotency.â€¢ odoo.get_sales_summary: Aggregate partner revenue over rolling windows (30/90/365 days).â€¢ odoo.points_adjust: Sync myCred balance to Odoo and apply corrective entries (if needed).â€¢ woo.get_order: Retrieve Woo order lines and amounts for points/commission rules.â€¢ drive.search_docs: Access policy tables and partner contracts (for decisions/escalations).â€¢ drive.append_note: Write audit entries for tier changes, payouts, and disputes.â€¢ monday.create_item: Update management boards: Partner KPIs, onboarding, incidents.â€¢ crm.create_ticket: Open support/dispute tickets related to partner payouts or tiers.6) Automation Flows (n8n + Zapier)Internal (n8n) Flows:1) Partner Onboarding   Trigger: Registration form submission (role=dealer/stand/affiliate).   Steps: Validate â†’ Create/Update Odoo partner â†’ Assign tier/pricelist â†’ Welcome email â†’ Create Monday item â€œOnboardingâ€.2) Points Awarding   Trigger: Order delivered.   Steps: Map SKU rules â†’ Calculate base &amp; bonus points â†’ Update myCred â†’ Mirror Odoo points via odoo.points_adjust â†’ Log to Drive.3) Affiliate Commission   Trigger: SliceWP conversion approved.   Steps: Compute commission (net order value per policy) â†’ odoo.create_payout(external_id='aff:{conv_id}') â†’ Email summary to finance.4) Stand Reconciliation   Trigger: Weekly schedule.   Steps: Compare stand sales vs. stock transfers â†’ Generate variance report â†’ Escalate discrepancies via CRM ticket.5) Tier Review   Trigger: Monthly.   Steps: odoo.get_sales_summary(90d) â†’ Evaluate policy thresholds â†’ odoo.update_partner_tier â†’ Notify partner â†’ Log to Drive.External (Zapier) Flows:â€¢ Communication: Send partner notifications (welcome/tier change/payout) via Gmail/WhatsApp Business.  â€¢ Marketing sync: Add top partners to co-marketing audiences (Meta/Google).  â€¢ Calendar events: Schedule quarterly partner reviews with management.7) Points &amp; Commission Rules (Policy)â€¢ Points (myCred):    â€“ Base points per â‚¬ spent; multipliers for tier and product category.    â€“ Bonus points for on-time payment and low return rates.    â€“ Expiry rules optional (e.g., 12-month inactivity).  â€¢ Affiliate Commissions (SliceWP):    â€“ Default % of net amount (order total â€“ VAT â€“ shipping â€“ discounts).    â€“ Exclusions: returns, fraud, staff orders; partial commissions for partial refunds.    â€“ Approval workflow before payout; disputes handled via CRM tickets.  â€¢ Dealer/Stand Bonuses:    â€“ Quarterly performance bonuses based on revenue and compliance score.    â€“ Extra rewards for new product launches or target achievements.  8) AI Reasoning &amp; Escalation1) Observe â†’ Register events: orders, conversions, transfers, and tickets.  2) Analyze â†’ Apply policy tables (tiers, commissions) from Drive; compare with historical behavior in Odoo.  3) Decide â†’ Calculate points/commissions or propose tier/payout changes.  4) Act â†’ Execute MCP tools (payouts, tier updates, points sync).  5) Reflect â†’ Write audit notes to Drive and summarize to Monday.  For exceptions (large payouts, tier downgrades), the AI seeks Hairo Assistant approval (HITL) before execution.9) KPIs &amp; DashboardsPrimary KPIs (reported to Monday):â€¢ Active partners (dealers/stands/affiliates).  â€¢ Partner revenue (rolling 30/90/365).  â€¢ Points awarded vs. redeemed.  â€¢ Commission payout amount and approval time.  â€¢ Tier distribution and movements (upgrades/downgrades).  â€¢ Dispute rate and resolution time.  Data exported weekly to Drive /AI_Reports/Partner_Programs/ for archival and analysis.10) Security &amp; Access Controlâ€¢ MCP scopes: partners.read, partners.write, payouts.write, points.write, drive.read/write, monday.write.  â€¢ Odoo service user: â€œAI_Partners_Botâ€ with limited access to res.partner, sale, account, stock.  â€¢ myCred &amp; SliceWP credentials stored in n8n secrets vault; rotated quarterly.  â€¢ PII redaction for AI context; audit trails include correlation_id and external_id.  â€¢ HITL for payouts above threshold (e.g., â‚¬1,000) and for tier downgrades.  11) Inter-Department Collaborationâ€¢ Sales AI â†’ provides revenue signals for tier evaluation and bonuses.  â€¢ Accounting AI â†’ validates payouts, posts credit notes for returns impacting commissions.  â€¢ Logistics AI â†’ supplies delivery &amp; return status affecting points and compliance scores.  â€¢ Marketing AI â†’ coordinates co-marketing with top-performing partners.  All interactions are routed through Hairo Assistant to enforce policy consistency and auditability.12) Learning &amp; Continuous Improvementâ€¢ Learns partner performance patterns (seasonality, product affinity).  â€¢ Adjusts bonus thresholds based on ROI and dispute trends.  â€¢ Maintains training dataset in Drive /AI_Training/Partner_Programs/.  â€¢ Quarterly â€œPartner Programs Intelligence Reportâ€ auto-generated for management review.13) Governanceâ€¢ Config stored in Drive (/Governance/AI_Agents/Partner_Programs/).  â€¢ Version Tag: AI-PARTNERS-v{major.minor}.  â€¢ Changes require AI Policy Board approval; staging tests via Odoo sandbox and SliceWP sandbox.  â€¢ Compliance with GDPR, GoBD; financial payouts reconciled in Odoo Accounting.  â€¢ Monthly review chaired by Hairo Assistant and Channel Lead.
